Originally Designed For Vive Wands\n- -\nFirearms use Trigger, 2Axis Input\nMovement uses Menu / B Button\nHas full complex control set of all weapon types\n--\nNot recommended for controllers that only have a single 2Axis input (touchpad OR joystick but not both) UNLESS you're using Teleport/Dash or Armswinger Movement=最初为Vive Wands设计\n- -\n枪械使用扳机，2轴输入\n使用菜单或B按钮移动\n拥有所有武器类型的完整复杂控制集\n--\n不推荐用于仅有单个2轴输入的控制器（触摸板或操纵杆，但不能同时使用），除非你使用传送/冲刺或摆臂移动方式

Vive/Rift: Click Menu/B/Y Button to activate locomotion on a hand. Primary 2axis inputs behave like a gamepad (and cannot use weapon functions while active). \n\nIndex/WMR: Joysticks behave like gamepad.\n\nNOTE: There is NO smooth turning available.\n\nGravity & Wall Collision are Enabled.=Vive/Rift：单击菜单/B/Y按钮激活这支手的移动控制。主要2轴输入的行为类似于游戏手柄（并且在激活时无法使用武器功能）。\n\nIndex/WMR：摇杆的行为类似于游戏手柄。\n\n注意：无法使用平滑转向。\n\n重力和墙壁碰撞已启用。
Click Menu/B/Y Button to activate locomotion on a hand. This hand now moves you (and cannot use weapon functions while active).\n\nPress primary 2axis input (touchpad/joystick) forward/up and hold.\n\nDrag input to the side to make arrow at end of arc turn. Release input to teleport.\n\nGravity & Wall Collision are Disabled=单击菜单/B/Y按钮激活这支手的移动控制。这只手现在会移动你（而且激活时无法使用武器功能）。\n\n向前/向上按下主要2轴输入（触摸板/操纵杆）并按住。\n\n将输入拖到一侧可使弧线末端的箭头转动。释放输入即可传送。\n\n重力和墙壁碰撞已禁用
Click-Hold Menu/B/Y Buttons while swinging that controller (in any direction) to increase speed.\n\nThe direction your controller is pointed controls which way you go. If you hold both controller buttons the direction is averaged. \n\nPunching both hands upward while holding buttons is jump!\n\nGravity & Wall Collision are Disabled=按住菜单/B/Y按钮并摆动控制器（朝任意方向）可提高速度。\n\n控制器指向的方向控制着你的前进方向。如果你同时按住两个控制器按钮，则方向会取平均。\n\n按住按钮的同时双手向上挥动就能跳跃！\n\n重力和墙壁碰撞已禁用

Greetings!\n\nIf you're new to H3, click through the entries on the left there to get a quick start on things, or click a section on the top bar to spawn some toys to play with!\n\nIf you need help with something there are several helpful links to the left, clicking on them will copy the url to your clip board, which you can paste into a web browser to find more info, or join one of our helpful communities!\n\nAll of us here at RUST LTD. hope you have a Wonderful time!=欢迎！\n\n如果你是H3新手，请点击左侧的条目快速上手，或点击顶栏上的一个部分来生成一些玩具来玩！\n\n如果你需要帮助，左侧有几个有用的链接，点击它们会将URL复制到你的剪贴板，你可以将其粘贴到浏览器中以查找更多信息，或者加入我们的乐于助人的社区之一！\n\nRUST LTD的全体同仁希望你度过愉快的时光！

Click on Top Bar buttons to go to their various pages.\r\n\nEach page will save your selection and tags until you load into a different scene or reload the current scene.\r\n\nThis Spawner is still under construction so some pages may be incomplete or missing.\r=单击顶部栏按钮可转到其各个页面。\r\n\n每个页面都会保存你的选择和标签，直到你加载到不同的场景或重新加载当前场景。\r\n\n此生成器仍在建设中，因此某些页面可能不完整或缺失。\r
Click on the FIREARMS button on the Top Bar.\r\n\nUse the Tag categories section on the left to narrow things down.\r\n\nClick on Gun icons to select them, then, in the right most panel, click the SPAWN button and your gun will appear.\r\n=点击顶部栏上的“枪支”按钮。\r\n\n使用左侧的标签类别部分缩小范围。\r\n\n点击枪支图标进行选择，然后在最右侧面板中点击“生成”按钮，你的枪支就会出现。\r\n
You can Click the SPAWN AMMO PANEL button right on this page.\n\nYou can also click on the AMMO button on the Top Bar to see all Ammo, Magazines, Speedloaders and Stripper Clips available in game.\r\n\nThe Ammo page uses similar Tag sorting to Firearms.\r\r=你可以单击此页面上的“生成弹药面板”按钮。\n\n你还可以单击顶部栏上的“弹药”按钮查看游戏中所有可用的弹药、弹匣、快速装弹器和桥夹。\r\n\n弹药页面使用与枪支类似的标签排序。\r\r
You can SPAWNLOCK ammo, magazines, speedloaders, and clips.\r\n1. Place the object in one of your Quickbelt slots.\r\n2. Hover your empty hand over the slot.\r\n3. Click the B button, the slot will turn blue.\r\n4. You can now take copies of that object out of the slot.\r\n5. Check the HELP section for more detailed Spawnlocking mechanics.\r\n=你可以生成锁定弹药、弹匣、快速装弹器和弹夹。\r\n1. 将物体放入你的快捷腰带插槽之一。\r\n2. 将空手悬停在插槽上。\r\n3. 单击B按钮，插槽将变为蓝色。\r\n4. 你现在可以从插槽中复制该物体。\r\n5. 查看帮助部分以获取更详细的生成锁定机制。\r\n
Pretty much all guns shoot by pulling the trigger.\r\nYou might have to do something else first to ready the gun though.\r\nMake sure if your gun has a safety it is disengaged.\r\nThis is done by clicking the B button. You should hear a click.\r\nAlso make sure you've got a round chambered!\r\nVisit the Sample Platter scene for an Intro to common gun controls.\r=几乎所有枪支都是通过扣动扳机来射击的。\r\n不过，你可能必须先做些其他事情来准备好枪支。\r\n如果你的枪支有保险装置，确保保险装置已解除。\r\n这可以通过按下B按钮来完成。你应该会听到咔嗒声。\r\n同时确保你已经装好子弹！\r\n访问“样本拼盘”场景，了解常见枪支控制的介绍。\r

You Have a (hard to find) Windows 11 Setting Wrong\nAnd It Will Make H3 Run Like Garbage!\nYou NEED to enable Optimizations for windowed games in Windows 11\n\nThe Button Below will change this setting and close H3 (it needs to be opened again after)\nIf somehow this DOESN'T fix it, you need to go enable the setting yourself.\nIt is Found in Start -> Settings -> System -> Display -> \nGraphics -> Change Default Graphics Settings\nSelect the Setting under Optimizations for windows games to turn it ON.\n\nThen Run H3 Again.=你有个（很难找到的）Windows 11的设置有误\n这将导致H3运行异常！\n你需要在 Windows 11中启用“窗口化游戏优化”\n\n下面的按钮将更改此设置并关闭H3（之后需要手动再次打开游戏）\n如果此操作无法解决问题，你需要自行启用该设置。\n它位于“开始”->“设置”->“系统”->“屏幕”->\n“显示卡”->“更改默认图形设置”\n选择“窗口化游戏优化”将其启用。\n\n然后再次运行 H3。

It looks like your controllers are stuck in the ground! \n\nDo you still need to turn them on?\n\nIf you've turned them on, SteamVR can see them, and they're still down there,\nsomething is broken!\n\nThe most common causes of this are:\n\n- You installed VR Perf Kit (this breaks H3, you need to remove it)\n- You have old/broken mods causing init failure (plz fix them)\n- H3 install is corrupted (try reinstalling it)\n- Oculus runtime / SteamVR are borked (try reinstalling those?)\n\nIf NONE of this fixes your problem, make a post in the Steam Forum\nBug Reports section of the H3 Steam Community and we'll help ya out!=看起来你的控制器卡在地上了！\n\n你是否开启了它们的电源？\n\n如果你已经打开它们，且在SteamVR可以看到它们，但它们仍然卡在地里，\n一定有什么地方坏了！\n\n最常见的原因是：\n\n- 你安装了VRPerfKit（这会破坏H3，你需要将其移除）\n- 你安装了旧的/损坏的模组导致初始化失败（请修复它们）\n- 游戏文件已损坏（尝试重新安装）\n- Oculus运行时/SteamVR已损坏（尝试重新安装它们？）\n\n如果这些都无法解决你的问题，请在H3 Steam社区的Steam论坛\nBug报告部分发帖，我们会帮助你！

READ THIS FIRST!!!!!!\n\nRogue-like Permadeath: \n\nYOU _WILL_ DIE.\n\nWhen you die or close the game, you lose all of your items, guns, and ammo!!\n\nQuests you complete for NPCS and the rewards NPCs give you are _Permanent_ though. Just swing by their location to get new stuff each run! \n\nAlso, Equipment Cases bought in Stores are always permanent too! Each run you'll get another new semi-random item of the type (ex. Pistol carbine) in that case.\n\n=请先阅读此内容！！！！！！\n\n类Rogue的永久死亡模式：\n\n你_会_死。\n\n当你死亡或关闭游戏时，你将失去所有物品、枪支和弹药！！\n\n不过，你为NPC完成的任务以及NPC给予你的奖励是_永久_的。每次游戏只需前往他们的位置即可获得新物品！\n\n此外，在商店购买的装备箱也是永久的！每次游戏你都会在装备箱中获得另一个新的同类型的半随机物品（例如卡宾枪）。\n\n

It's your job to breach and clear the hotel. There are several points of access, including breakable windows, and rappel points on either side of the building. Greetings!\n\nWelcome to the Portable Item Spawner! We've got a couple usability things to cover super quick on it:\n\n1. This sucker is a pretty complex object. Its display turns off when in a quickbelt, so if you need to use it in a bunch of places, and get stutters while moving, pop it in a slot before moving!\n\n2. Yes, the text is tiny. That's what happens when you cram a 2ish meter display down to something portable :-P But we did this at request, and knowing the modder folk would just do it -anyway- if we didn't. Just know this wasn't reeeeeeeally design for portability.\n\n3. Use the Stylus on the side for spawning objects (from details pane, or Save/Load). Just point it at a spot and click the trigger while holding the Stylus. Similarly you can use the Stylus to scan objects to save by pointing at them and hitting the Scan button.\n\nAll of us here at RUST LTD. hope you have a Wonderful time!=您好！\n\n欢迎使用便携式物品生成器！我们有几个可用性方面的问题需要快速介绍一下：\n\n1. 这个东西相当复杂。当它被挂在快捷腰带上时，显示屏会关闭，所以如果你需要在很多地方使用它，并且在移动时会卡顿，请在移动前把它插到插槽里！\n\n2. 是的，文字很小。这就是当你把一个2米左右的显示屏塞进便携式设备时会发生的情况 :-P 但我们是应要求这么做的，而且我们知道即使我们不这么做，模组制作者也会这么做。要知道，这真的不是专为便携性设计的。\n\n3. 使用侧面的触控笔来生成物体（从详细信息窗格，或保存/加载）。只需将其指向一个点，然后在握住触控笔的同时点击扳机即可。同样，您可以使用触控笔扫描要保存的对象，只需指向它们并点击扫描按钮即可。\n\nRUST LTD 的全体同仁祝您度过愉快的时光！

Nuclear option. If true, deletes the cache on the next start of H3VR. The cache will be built from scratch. This takes the most time and the most RAM to finish. This setting will always be set back to false after startup.\nDefault Value: False=核弹选项。如果设置为 true，则在下次启动 H3VR 时删除缓存。缓存将从头开始构建。这将耗费最多的时间和内存。此设置在启动后始终会恢复为 false。\n默认值：False

Tutorial: (1) Place gun on QB slot (2) Select camo pack and type (3) Select unlocked camo, 'APPLY Camo' (4) Select locked camo (5) Pick any challenge, 'Accept Challenge' on gun.\n\nRules: (1) Progress tracks only on challenge's bound gun (2) Each gun can unlock a max of 5 camos (3) 'Remove' uncompleted challenges from a gun to replace it with another.=教程：(1) 将枪放在 QB 槽 (2) 选择迷彩包并输入 (3) 选择未锁定的迷彩，“应用迷彩” (4) 选择锁定的迷彩 (5) 选择任意挑战，在枪上“接受挑战”。\n\n规则：(1) 进度轨道仅在挑战绑定的枪上 (2) 每把枪最多可以解锁 5 个迷彩 (3) 从枪上“移除”未完成的挑战，用另一把枪替换。
